***verliezen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verliezen.html>verliezen</a> (812)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verliesen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*firliosan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fraleusaną</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">verlieren</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λύω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lúō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">loose, untie</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">solvō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dissolve</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">forlorn</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verliezen.html>verliezen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to lose <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">possession</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to lose (a game), to be defeated</li></ol>

***verlopen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verlopen.html>verlopen</a> (4794)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verlôpen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>lopen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verlopen.html>verlopen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to progress</li>
<li>to expire, to become invalid</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colors</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fade</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">clocks</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go fast/slow, to go out of pace
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:klokken.html>Klokken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:standaard.html>standaard</a> computersystemen <b><a href = vnd.unilang:verlopen.html>verlopen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> 2 <a href = vnd.unilang:seconden.html>seconden</a> per 6 <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> 7 <a href = vnd.unilang:minuten.html>minuten</a>.</i> <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://74.125.153.132/search?q=cache:2-Fc-LIVefkJ:handle.dtic.mil/100.2/ADA311584+verlopen+definitionamp;cd=20amp;hl=zh-TWamp;ct=clnkamp;gl=tw">[1]</a>
<dl><dd>Standard computer system clocks can be up to two <a href = vnd.unilang:seconds.html>seconds</a> off per six to seven minutes.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verlossen.html>verlossen</a> (8471)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:los.html>los</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>, or <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lossen.html>lossen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verlossen.html>verlossen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>To free (of something).</li>
<li>To redeem.</li>
<li>To attend the birth of an infant and provide postpartum care to the mother and her infant.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verloving.html>verloving</a> (7902)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verloven.html>verloven</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">affiance</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ment</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verloving.html>verloving</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verlovingen.html>verlovingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verloving.html>verlovinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span>

***vermeerderen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vermeerderen.html>vermeerderen</a> (44423)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meerder.html>meerder</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vermeerderen.html>vermeerderen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to increase in number, to multiply</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to increase in number, to multiply</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:vermicelli.html>vermicelli</a></i>, plural of <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">vermicello</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">little worm</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">verme</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">worm</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:vermis.html>vermis</a></i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">-cello</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">diminutive <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***vernachelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vernachelen.html>vernachelen</a> (86690)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vernachelen.html>vernachelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to con, to scam, to deceive</li>

***vernederen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vernederen.html>vernederen</a> (8045)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:neder.html>neder</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">down</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vernederen.html>vernederen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to humiliate, humble</li>
<li>(<i>reflexive use: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vernederen.html>vernederen</a></b></i>) to stoop to, humble/humiliate oneself
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vernederde.html>vernederde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:blote.html>blote</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:knie.html>knieën</a> starf <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vergiffenis.html>vergiffenis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vragen.html>vragen</a></i>
<dl><dd>He humbled himself by begging on naked knees for punshment and forgiveness</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

***vernederend.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vernederend.html>vernederend</a> (7706)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vernederend.html>vernederend</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vernederend.html>vernederender</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">vernederendst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>humiliating, constituting or implying humiliation</li></ol>

***vernemen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vernemen.html>vernemen</a> (23285)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vernēmen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">farneman</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*franemaną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nemen.html>nemen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vernemen.html>vernemen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to learn (of), to find out, to hear (about)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>Dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vernomen.html>vernomen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Palestijnse <a href = vnd.unilang:artsen.html>artsen</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> This (information) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>learnt</b> from Palestinian <a href = vnd.unilang:doctors.html>doctors</a>.</dd></dl></li></ol>
